CREATE TABLE IL_Comcast (
  ID int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  ItemNumber varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  CustomerName varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  City varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  State varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  Qty float DEFAULT NULL,
  ExtCost float DEFAULT NULL,
  Vendor varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  Division varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  Month varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  ProdType varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  ProdCategory varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  Year int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  KEY tbl_Comcastind_year (Year)
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_ESTTABLE (
  TITLE varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  CONTACT varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  CUSTCODE varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  CUSTNAME varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  CustomerName varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  COUNTRY varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  STATE varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  EMAILADD varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  FAX varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  PHONE varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  STATUS varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  ESTIMATETYPE varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  SALESREP varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  PODATE datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  DUEDATE datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  STARTDATE datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  COMPLETEDATE datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  MATNAME varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  USER1 varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  EstimatesId bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  podate_percent bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  ontime_percent bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  total_days bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  QUOTE_COUNT bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  Total_SmallValue decimal(28,12) DEFAULT NULL,
  Total_LargeValue decimal(28,12) DEFAULT NULL
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_DataSource (
DataSource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded' ,
Datasource_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key + PK' ,
Datasource_Name VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Name of the Datasource' ,
DataSource_Descr VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Description of the datasource' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX DataSource_idx_Key(Datasource_Key)
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- Master Date table holds all the dates information.
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IL_Date (
Date_Val DATE  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Holds the date' ,
Date_Key INTEGER UNSIGNED  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate key' ,
Day_Of_Month INTEGER UNSIGNED  NULL   COMMENT 'Field will hold day number of Month' ,
Day_Name VARCHAR(20)  NULL   COMMENT 'Contains name of the day, Sunday, Monday' ,
Day_Of_week INTEGER UNSIGNED  NULL   COMMENT 'First Day Sunday=1 and Saturday=7' ,
Week_Of_Year INTEGER UNSIGNED  NULL   COMMENT 'Week of the Year' ,
Calendar_Month INTEGER UNSIGNED  NULL   COMMENT 'Number of the Month 1 to 12' ,
Calendar_Month_Name VARCHAR(20)  NULL   COMMENT 'January, February etc' ,
Calendar_Year INTEGER UNSIGNED  NULL   COMMENT 'Year value of Date stored in Row' ,
Calendar_Yrmo INTEGER UNSIGNED  NULL   COMMENT 'holds 201301,201302' ,
Calendar_Quarter INTEGER UNSIGNED  NULL   COMMENT 'Q1 , Q2,Q3,Q4 querters for the date' ,
Fiscal_Month INTEGER UNSIGNED  NULL   COMMENT 'Fiscal Month detail' ,
Fiscal_Yrmo INTEGER UNSIGNED  NULL   COMMENT 'Fiscal month year 201304' ,
Fiscal_Quarter INTEGER UNSIGNED  NULL   COMMENT 'Fiscal Quarter details' ,
Fiscal_Year INTEGER UNSIGNED  NULL   COMMENT 'Fiscal year detail' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT '0 for active record and 1 for inactive record.' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Date_Val)  ,
INDEX IL_Date_Date_Key(Date_Key)  ,
INDEX IL_Date_IDX_Cal_Mnth(Calendar_Month)  ,
INDEX IL_Date_IDX_Mnth_Name(Calendar_Month_Name)  ,
INDEX IL_Date_Cal_Year(Calendar_Year)  ,
INDEX IL_Date_Idx_Yrmo(Calendar_Yrmo)  ,
INDEX IL_Date_Idx_Quarter(Calendar_Quarter)  ,
INDEX IL_Date_Idx_Week_Yr(Week_Of_Year))
ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;
CREATE TABLE IL_Region (
Region VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Uniquely identfied Region Name' ,
Region_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key + PK' ,
Region_Code BIGINT  NULL   COMMENT 'Code of the Region' ,
Region_Desc VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Description of the Region' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'If Active 0 else 1' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Region)  ,
INDEX IL_Region_RegionKey(Region_Key)
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;
CREATE TABLE IL_Dashboard (
Dashboard_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key + PK' ,
Module_Name VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Name of the Dashobard Module' ,
KPI_Name VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Name of the KPI that need to set the Threshold' ,
Mesure_Type VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Type of measurement ex: % or $' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Is active KPI then 0 else 1' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Dashboard_Key)
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

Company_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL  ,

BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,

)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IL_Currency (
Currency_Code VARCHAR(10)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Currency code detail' ,
Currency_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key' ,
Currency_Name VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Currency description' ,
Symbol TEXT  NULL   COMMENT 'Symbol of the Currency' ,
Decimal_Digit BIGINT  NULL   COMMENT 'Decimal Digit maintained for Dashboard to show.' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT '0 for active record and 1 for inactive record.' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Currency_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_Currency_Curr_Id(Currency_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_Currency_CurrKey(Currency_Key))
ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_Product_Group (
Prod_Grp_ID VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Source Product code or group id' ,
Product_Grp_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key' ,
Prod_Grp_Code VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Product Group code details' ,
Prod_Grp_Desc VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Product description details' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT '0 for active record and 1 for inactive record.' ,
BCharacter01 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BCharacter02 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber01 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BDateTime01 DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BBoolean BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Prod_Grp_ID)  ,
INDEX IL_Product_Grp_Idx_Key(Product_Grp_Key)  ,
INDEX IL_Product_Grp_idx_Code(Prod_Grp_Code))
ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- Holds the Master  Status details of Order/Inventory/PO/Shipment etc
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IL_Status  (
Status_Code VARCHAR(20)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Status Code or ID followed in source system' ,
Status_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate key' ,
Status_Descr VARCHAR(20)  NULL   COMMENT 'Description of the status' ,
Status_Group VARCHAR(20)  NULL   COMMENT 'Category or group managed in Source' ,
Rpt_Valid_Flag BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Is valid to show this status code data in Report then 0 else 1' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT '0 for active record and 1 for inactive record.' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Status_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_Status_Status_Code(Status_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_Status_StsKey(Status_Key))
ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- Holds the Master data for the  Line of the Product on the category
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IL_Product_Line (
Product_Line_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Source Product Line' ,
Product_Line_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'surrogate key' ,
Product_Line_Name VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Product Line Name' ,
Product_Line_Descr VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Product Line description' ,
Rpt_Valid_Flag BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Required to show the product line 0 else 1' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT '0 for active record and 1 for inactive record.' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Product_Line_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Product_Line_Key(Product_Line_Key))
ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;
CREATE TABLE IL_Client_Currency (
Client_Currency_Key BIGINT UNSIGNED  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key   + Auto Generated' ,
Client_Id VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Client Id as Defined in Anvizent Data Prep Tool' ,
Currency_Code VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Currency Code details for Base currency or Transactional Currency setup.' ,
Cmpny_Currency_Descr VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Description of the Currency' ,
Currency_Type VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Type of the Currency' ,
Order_Seq BIGINT ZEROFILL  NULL   COMMENT 'Order Seq  that need to be shown in Dashboard' ,
Rpt_Base_Currency_Flag BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'If Current Country code is a Base Currency the need to Set the Flag' ,
Symbol VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Symbol of the Currency' ,

CREATE TABLE IL_Country (
Country VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Source Country Id or code' ,
Currency_Code VARCHAR(10)  NULL   COMMENT 'Transactional Base Currency Code of the Country' ,
Country_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key + PK' ,

Country_Latitude VARCHAR(50)   NULL   COMMENT 'Geo Location Latitude details' ,
Country_Longitude VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Geo Location Longitude details' ,
Region VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Region of the Country' ,
Rpt_Valid_Flag BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Is valid to show this status code data in Report then 0 else 1' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT '0 for active record and 1 for inactive record.' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Country)  ,
INDEX IL_Country_Country_Code(Country)  ,
INDEX IL_Country_Country_Latitude(Country_Latitude)  ,
INDEX IL_Country_Country_Longitude(Country_Longitude)  ,
INDEX IL_Country_FKIndex1(Region)  ,
INDEX IL_Country_CountryKey(Country_Key)  ,
INDEX IL_Country_FKIndex2(Currency_Code),
FOREIGN KEY(Region)
REFERENCES IL_Region(Region)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Currency_Code)

ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION)
ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_Currency_Rate (
CURR_RATE_ID INTEGER UNSIGNED  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key' ,
From_Currency_Code VARCHAR(10)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'From Currency Code that Transaction set' ,
To_Currency_Code VARCHAR(10)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'To currency code that need to conversion applied' ,
EXCHANGE_RATE NUMERIC(18,10) ZEROFILL  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Average Exchange/Financial/Account rate for the Caluclation Period.' ,
CURRENCY_START_PERIOD DATETIME  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Start Date Period from Currecy  Rate changes' ,
CURRENCY_END_PERIOD DATETIME  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'End Date Period of Currecy  Rate changes valid' ,
RATE_FREQUENCY VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Plan to enter rates for the selected Exchange rate.' ,
CALUCLATION_TYPE VARCHAR(50)  NULL DEFAULT 'Multiply'  COMMENT 'Multiply or Divide  Default "Multiply"' ,
DataSource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded' ,
IS_LOCKED BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Currency entry will be locked fo previous period. Not allowed to update the currency record.This may impact DL tables data' ,
ADDED_USER VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
ADDED_DATE DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
UPDATED_DATE DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
UPDATED_USER VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(CURR_RATE_ID)  ,
INDEX IL_Currency_Rate_ExchangeRate(EXCHANGE_RATE)  ,
INDEX IL_Currency_Rate_StrtPerd(CURRENCY_START_PERIOD)  ,
INDEX IL_Currency_Rate_EndPerd(CURRENCY_END_PERIOD)  ,
INDEX IL_Currency_Rate_FKIndex1(From_Currency_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_Currency_Rate_FKIndex2(To_Currency_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_Currency_Rate_FKIndex3(DataSource_Id),
FOREIGN KEY(From_Currency_Code)
REFERENCES IL_Currency(Currency_Code)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(To_Currency_Code)
REFERENCES IL_Currency(Currency_Code)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_DataSource(DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,

Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or Sysdate' ,

-- ------------------------------------------------------------

CREATE TABLE IL_State (
State VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Source Region Id or code' ,
Country VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Geo Hierarchy mapping to country' ,
State_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key' ,
State_Name VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Name of the State' ,
State_Descr VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Description of the Region or State' ,
Currency_Code VARCHAR(10)  NULL   COMMENT 'Base Currency Code Details' ,
Rpt_Order_Seq BIGINT  NULL   COMMENT 'Order sequence of the State or Region need to show in report' ,
State_Latitude VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Geo Location Latitude details' ,
State_Longitude VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Geo Location Longitude details' ,
Rpt_Valid_Flag BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Is valid to show this status code data in Report then 0 else 1' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT '0 for active record and 1 for inactive record.' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)   NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(State, Country)  ,
INDEX IL_State_FKIndex1(Country)  ,
INDEX IL_State_StateKey(State_Key)  ,
INDEX IL_State_FKIndex2(Currency_Code),
FOREIGN KEY(Country)
REFERENCES IL_Country(Country)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Currency_Code)
REFERENCES IL_Currency(Currency_Code)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION)
ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_Supplier (
Supplier_ID VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Supplier/Vendor Id or Code from the source' ,

Supplier_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key' ,
XRef_Supplier_Key BIGINT  NULL  ,
Supplier_Name VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Supplier name details' ,
Supplier_Descr VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Name or Description of the Vendor or Supplier' ,
Supplier_Address1 VARCHAR(250)  NULL   COMMENT 'Supplier address' ,
Supplier_Address2 VARCHAR(250)  NULL   COMMENT 'Supplier address' ,
Supplier_City VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Supplier city' ,
State VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'State of the Supplier' ,
Country VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Country of the Supplier' ,
Supplier_Zipcode VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'supplier Postal code or Zipcode' ,
Supplier_Category VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'supply cateogry' ,
Phone_No VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Home or Office Ph number' ,
Fax_Num VARCHAR(50)   NULL   COMMENT 'Fax number details of the Supplier' ,
Email_Addr VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Email address of the supplier' ,
Home_Page VARCHAR(2000)  NULL   COMMENT 'Web site page of the Supplier' ,
Base_Currency_Code VARCHAR(10)  NULL  ,
Min_Order_Value NUMERIC(18,2) ZEROFILL  NULL  ,
Max_Order_Value NUMERIC(18,2) ZEROFILL  NULL  ,
Approver_Name VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
BCharacter01 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BCharacter02 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber01 NUMERIC(18,2) ZEROFILL  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2) ZEROFILL  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BDateTime01 DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BBoolean BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT '0 for active record and 1 for inactive record.' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Supplier_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Supplier_FKIndex2(Country)  ,
INDEX IL_Supplier_FKIndex3(State, Country)  ,
INDEX IL_Supplier_SupplierKey(Supplier_Key)  ,
INDEX IL_Supplier_FKIndex5(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Supplier_FKIndex4(DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Supplier_FKIndex6(Base_Currency_Code),
FOREIGN KEY(Country)
REFERENCES IL_Country(Country)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(State, Country)
REFERENCES IL_State(State, Country)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Company(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_DataSource(DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Base_Currency_Code)
REFERENCES IL_Currency(Currency_Code)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION)
ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_Plant (

Sub_Region VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Region location of the Plant' ,

Plant_Longitude VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Geo Location Longitude details' ,

BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BDateTime01 DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BBoolean BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT '0 for active record and 1 for inactive record.' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Plant_Idx_Plantkey(Plant_Key)  ,
INDEX IL_Plant_IdxPlantName(Plant_Name)  ,
INDEX IL_Plant_Idx_SubRegion(Sub_Region)  ,
INDEX IL_Plant_Idx_Latitude(Plant_Latitude)  ,
INDEX IL_Plant_Idx_Longitude(Plant_Longitude)  ,
INDEX IL_Plant_FKIndex2(Country)  ,
INDEX IL_Plant_FKIndex3(State, Country)  ,
INDEX IL_Plant_FKIndex4(Region)  ,
INDEX IL_Plant_FKIndex7(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Plant_FKIndex5(DataSource_Id),
FOREIGN KEY(Country)
REFERENCES IL_Country(Country)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(State, Country)
REFERENCES IL_State(State, Country)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Region)
REFERENCES IL_Region(Region)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Company(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_DataSource(DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION)

CREATE TABLE IL_Product (
Product_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Source Product ID details' ,
Company_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Company name of the Product' ,
DataSource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded' ,
Product_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key + PK' ,
XRef_Product_Key BIGINT  NULL  ,
Product_Code VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Product code' ,
Product_Name VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Name of the Product' ,
Prod_Desc VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Description of the Product' ,
ProductSpec VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Product Specification details' ,
Prod_Grp_ID VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Product Group or Caregory' ,
Prod_Sub_Grp_ID VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Product Sub Group or Caregory' ,
Product_Line_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Product Line Category' ,
Brand_Id VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'market brand codes to uniquely identify products and traded items' ,
Product_Height NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
Product_Length NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
Product_Width NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
Size_UOM VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Product_Weight NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
Weight_UOM VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
BCharacter01 VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BCharacter02 VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber01 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BDateTime01 DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BBoolean BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT '0 for active record and 1 for inactive record.' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Product_Idx_PrdKey(Product_Key)  ,
INDEX IL_Product_PrdCode(Product_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_Product_FKIndex2(Prod_Grp_ID)  ,
INDEX IL_Product_FKIndex3(Prod_Sub_Grp_ID)  ,
INDEX IL_Product_FKIndex4(Product_Line_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Product_FKIndex5(Brand_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Product_FKIndex7(DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Product_FKIndex6(Company_Id, DataSource_Id),
FOREIGN KEY(Prod_Grp_ID)
REFERENCES IL_Product_Group(Prod_Grp_ID)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Prod_Sub_Grp_ID)
REFERENCES IL_Product_Sub_Group(Prod_Sub_Grp_ID)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Product_Line_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Product_Line(Product_Line_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Brand_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Brand(Brand_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_DataSource(DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Company(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION)
ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_ProductPlant (
Company_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL  ,
Product_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL  ,
Plant_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL  ,
DataSource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL  ,

CREATE TABLE IL_Customer (
Customer_ID VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Source Customer Id or Code' ,
Company_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Company Id details' ,
DataSource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded' ,
Customer_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key' ,
XRef_Customer_Key BIGINT  NULL  ,
Customer_Name VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Customer Name' ,
Address1 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Customer address details' ,
Address2 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Customer address details' ,
City VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Customer city details' ,
State VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'State of the Customer located' ,
Country VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Country of the Customer Located' ,
Zip_Code VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Customer postal code details' ,
Email_Addr VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Email address of the customer' ,
Cust_Category_id VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Customer category details' ,
Customer_Latitude VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Geo Location Latitude details' ,
Customer_Longitude VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Geo Location Longitude details' ,
Sales_Rep_Code VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Sales  Representive code that Customer Allocated' ,
Sales_Territory_Id VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Territory code that Sales Representive Located' ,
Region VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Region location of the company' ,
Sub_Region VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Region location of the company' ,
Currency_Code VARCHAR(10)  NULL   COMMENT 'Base Currency Code that Customer for Transaction' ,
Hierarchy_Lvl1 VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Hierarchy Lvl defined on client Project' ,
Hierarchy_Lvl2 VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Hierarchy Lvl defined on client Project' ,
Hierarchy_Lvl3 VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Hierarchy Lvl defined on client Project' ,
Hierarchy_Lvl4 VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Hierarchy Lvl defined on client Project' ,
EDI_Code VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Electronic Device Id' ,
Seed_Cust_Flag BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Dummy Customer or valid customer (0 for valid 1 for dummy)' ,
IsActive BIT  NULL   COMMENT '0 for active record and 1 for inactive record.' ,
Effective_Start_date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Applicable for SCD2 effective start date transaction' ,
Effective_End_date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Applicable for SCD2 effective end date transaction' ,
BCharacter01 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BCharacter02 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber01 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BDateTime01 DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BBoolean BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_Idx_CusKey(Customer_Key)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_Idx_custname(Customer_Name)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_Idx_CustLatitude(Customer_Latitude)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_Idx_CustLongitu(Customer_Longitude)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_Idx_SubRegion(Sub_Region)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_idx_effstart_dt(Effective_Start_date)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_Idx_EffEndDt(Effective_End_date)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_FKIndex2(State, Country)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_FKIndex3(Country)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_FKIndex4(Sales_Rep_Code, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_FKIndex5(Sales_Territory_Id, State, Country)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_FKRegion(Region)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_FKCurrCode(Currency_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_FKIndex7(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Customer_FKIndex8(DataSource_Id),
FOREIGN KEY(State, Country)
REFERENCES IL_State(State, Country)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Country)
REFERENCES IL_Country(Country)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Sales_Rep_Code, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_SalesRep(Sales_Rep_Code, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Sales_Territory_Id, State, Country)
REFERENCES IL_Territory(Territory_Id, State, Country)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Region)
REFERENCES IL_Region(Region)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Currency_Code)
REFERENCES IL_Currency(Currency_Code)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Company(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_DataSource(DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION)
ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

  Batch_Type varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Batch_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Batch_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Account_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Account_type varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Acct_Cat_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  COA_Code varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  GL_Account_Code varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Current_Account_Flag bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Acctount_Mode varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Plant_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  AP_Invoice_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  GL_Debit_Amount decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  AR_Invoice_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,

  Offset_GL_Code varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Reverse_Void_Code varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Fiscal_Year int(10) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  Fiscal_Period bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  Amount decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Product_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Ordered_Qty decimal(24,7) DEFAULT NULL,
  UOM_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Supplier_Id varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  Customer_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Payment_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Ledger_Checked_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Check_Cleared_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Supplier_Invoice_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  GL_Acct_Segment_Val1 varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  GL_Acct_Segment_Val2 varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  GL_Source_Module varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Supp_Invoice_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Base_Currency_Code varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Transaction_Currency_Code varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Exchange_Rate decimal(24,12) DEFAULT NULL,
  Receipt_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Registration_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,

  Bcharacter02 varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  BNumber01 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  BNumber02 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  BDateTime01 datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  BBoolean bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Added_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Added_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  Updated_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Updated_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (Company_Id,Voucher_Type,Voucher_Number,Voucher_Line_Number,Voucher_Date,Ledger_Type,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Account_Ledger_keyindex (Acct_Ledger_Key),
  KEY IL_Account_Ledger_FKIndex1 (DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Account_Ledger_FKIndex2 (Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Account_Ledger_FKIndex3 (Plant_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Account_Ledger_FKIndex4 (Product_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Account_Ledger_FKIndex5 (UOM_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY Supplier_Id (Supplier_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  CONSTRAINT IL_Account_Ledger_ibfk_1 FOREIGN KEY (DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_DataSource (DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Account_Ledger_ibfk_2 FOREIGN KEY (Supplier_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Supplier (Supplier_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Account_Ledger_ibfk_3 FOREIGN KEY (Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Plant (Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Account_Ledger_ibfk_4 FOREIGN KEY (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Product (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Account_Ledger_ibfk_5 FOREIGN KEY (UOM_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Unit_Of_Measurement (UOM_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

INDEX IL_Bookings_Goal_FKIndex7(Currency_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_Bookings_Goal_FKIndex5(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- Holds the Order Detailed transactions on Products with the line number.
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IL_Order_Dtl (
  Order_Number varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Unique sales order identification number in source.',
  Order_LineNumber varchar(15) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Order Serial number for multiple order else default 1',
  Company_Id varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Company of the SO placed',
  DataSource_Id varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded',
  Order_Type varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Type of the Order',
  Order_Dtl_Key bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key + Auto Increment',
  Plant_Id varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Plant id that order got Allocated',
  Warehouse_ID varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Warehouse details that stock are available.',
  Customer_ID varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Customer Code of the SO.',
  Cust_Ship_Addr_Id varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Shipment address of the Customer',
  Product_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Product Code / Item code details.',
  UOM_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Ordered_Qty decimal(24,7) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Quantity ordered per product.',
  Unit_Price decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Selling price of a single product.',
  Unit_Price_Discount decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Discounted cost price per unit for the Product',
  Order_Line_Amount decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Unit Price * Order Qty',
  Order_Line_Discount_Amount decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Unit Price Discount * Order Qty',
  Order_Line_Total_Amount decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Total Order Amount After discount  Order amount - Order discount amount',
  Order_Line_Status varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Status of the Order',
  Ordered_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Ordered Date',
  Shipped_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Shippment date for the order',
  Due_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Expected to delivery date to customer',
  Quote_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Quote_Line_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Sales_Category_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Misc_Amount decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Base_Price decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Avg_Price decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Last_Price decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Requested_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Requested Date of SO',
  Shipped_Qty decimal(24,7) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Shipped quantity for the order',
  Cancelled_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Order Cancel Date',
  Cancelled_Qty decimal(24,7) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Number of Qty Cancelled',
  Retruned_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Date of the product Returned.',
  Returned_Qty decimal(24,7) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Retruned Quantity of the Product',
  Back_Order_Qty decimal(24,7) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Back Order Qty',
  On_Hold_Qty decimal(24,7) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Hold Qty of the Product',
  Open_Qty decimal(24,7) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Order Line Open Quantity of the Product',
  MTS_Flag bit(1) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'To Identify the MTS and MTO SO details',
  Transport_Mode varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Mode of the Transport',
  Container_Id varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Container details',
  Reason_Code varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Reason Code for Hold or Cancel the order.',
  Transaction_Cur_Code varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Tranaction Currency  Code of the SO',
  Exchange_Rate decimal(24,7) DEFAULT NULL,
  Base_Curr_Code varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Base Currency Code of the SO',
  Gross_Weight decimal(18,5) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Weight of the Product in Gross',
  Measure_Weight varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'UOM of the Weight',
  EDI_Order_Number varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Electronic Data Interchange Order Number',
  BCharacter01 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BCharacter02 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber01 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber02 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BDateTime01 datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BBoolean bit(1) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  Added_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record insert/created date or sysdate',
  Added_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Added user',
  Updated_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate',
  Updated_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Updated user',
  PRIMARY KEY (Order_Number,Order_LineNumber,Company_Id,DataSource_Id,Order_Type),
  KEY IL_Order_Dtl_FKIndex2 (Customer_ID,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Order_Dtl_FKIndex3 (Cust_Ship_Addr_Id,Company_Id,Customer_ID,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Order_Dtl_FKIndex4 (Product_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Order_Dtl_OrdrDtlKey (Order_Dtl_Key),
  KEY IL_Order_Dtl_FKIndex5 (Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Order_Dtl_FKIndex6 (Warehouse_ID,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Order_Dtl_FKIndex7 (DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Order_Dtl_FKIndex8 (UOM_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Order_Dtl_FKIndex9 (Quote_Number,Quote_Line_Number,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Dtl_ibfk_1 FOREIGN KEY (Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Customer (Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Dtl_ibfk_2 FOREIGN KEY (Cust_Ship_Addr_Id, Company_Id, Customer_ID, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Cust_Shipping_Address (Cust_Ship_Addr_Id, Company_Id, Customer_ID, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Dtl_ibfk_3 FOREIGN KEY (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Product (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Dtl_ibfk_4 FOREIGN KEY (Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Company (Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Dtl_ibfk_5 FOREIGN KEY (Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Warehouse (Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Dtl_ibfk_6 FOREIGN KEY (DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_DataSource (DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Dtl_ibfk_7 FOREIGN KEY (UOM_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Unit_Of_Measurement (UOM_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Dtl_ibfk_8 FOREIGN KEY (Quote_Number, Quote_Line_Number, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Quote_Dtl (Quote_Number, Quote_Line_Number, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci COMMENT='Holds the Order Detailed transactions on Products with the line number.';

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- Holds Sales header order Transation data on Day basis for the customer,Plant and sales person basis.
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IL_Order_Hdr (
Order_Number VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Unique sales order identification number in source.' ,
Company_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Company code of the Order received' ,
DataSource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded' ,
Order_Hdr_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key + Auto Increment' ,
Order_Type VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Type of the SO' ,
Currency_Code VARCHAR(10)  NULL   COMMENT 'Type of the Currency Transaction done.' ,
Order_Status VARCHAR(20)  NULL   COMMENT 'Status of the Order' ,
Plant_ID VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Plant details that SO is allocated' ,
Sales_Rep_Code VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Sales representive Code of the Order booked' ,
Customer_ID VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Customer Code of the SO' ,
Contact_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Customer Enquired Date.' ,
Requested_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Date of the Order Requested' ,
Order_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Dates the sales order was CREATEd.' ,
Due_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Expected to delivery date to customer' ,
Cancelled_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Cancell date of the Order' ,
Total_Order_Amount NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Sales order Amount' ,
Total_Discount NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Total discount amount' ,
EDI_Order_Number VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Electronic Data Interchange Order number' ,
Online_Order_Flag BIT  NULL   COMMENT '0 = Order placed by sales person. 1 = Order placed online by customer.' ,
Comments VARCHAR(2000)  NULL   COMMENT 'Comments made by the sales representative or Customer' ,
BCharacter01 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BCharacter02 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,

Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Order_Number, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Order_Hdr_FKIndex2(Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Order_Hdr_FKIndex3(Plant_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Order_Hdr_FKIndex4(Order_Status)  ,
INDEX IL_Order_Hdr_FKIndex8(Sales_Rep_Code, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Order_Hdr_OrderHdrKey(Order_Hdr_Key)  ,
INDEX IL_Order_Hdr_FKIndex5(Currency_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_Order_Hdr_FKIndex6(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Order_Hdr_FKIndex7(DataSource_Id),
FOREIGN KEY(Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Customer(Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Plant_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Plant(Plant_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,

REFERENCES IL_Status (Status_Code)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,

ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,

REFERENCES IL_Currency(Currency_Code)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,

ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION)
ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;
CREATE TABLE IL_Logistics (
Logistic_Id VARCHAR(100)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Uniquely identifed Logistic Number' ,
Company_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Sales Ordered Company Id' ,
Order_Number VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'SO line Number' ,
Order_LineNumber VARCHAR(15)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'SO Number' ,
DataSource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded' ,
Order_Type VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL  ,
Logistic_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key + PK' ,
Plant_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Plant Id of the SO That recived the Order' ,
Warehouse_ID VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Warehouse or Product Line  Details where Product picked up.' ,
Product_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Product that picked up and delivered to Customer or distributer' ,
Track_Number VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Track Number of Shipping Goods' ,
Primary_Srvc_Provider_Id VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Primary Service provider or Supplier details to shipp the product to Customer' ,
Delivery_Status VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Status of the Delivery' ,
Shipping_Type VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Type of Shippement Ex: Regular or Premium' ,
PickedUp_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Date of the good picked up from Warehouse/Branch' ,
Due_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Due Date to deliver it to customer' ,
Delivered_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Date of delivery to Customer' ,
PickedUp_Qty NUMERIC(24,7)  NULL   COMMENT 'Goods or product picked up Quantity' ,
Delivered_Qty NUMERIC(24,7)  NULL   COMMENT 'Goods or product Delivered Quantity' ,
Logistic_Cost NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Total logistic cost for the Goods or Product' ,
UOM_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
BCharacter01 VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BCharacter02 VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber01 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BDateTime01 DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BBoolean BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Logistic_Id, Company_Id, Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, DataSource_Id, Order_Type)  ,
INDEX IL_Logistics_FKIndex1(Primary_Srvc_Provider_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Logistics_FKIndex2(DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Logistics_FKIndex3(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Logistics_FKIndex4(Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type)  ,
INDEX IL_Logistics_FKIndex5(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Logistics_FKIndex6(Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Logistics_IdxLogistckey(Logistic_Key)  ,
INDEX IL_Logistics_FKIndex7(UOM_Id, DataSource_Id),
FOREIGN KEY(Primary_Srvc_Provider_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Service_Provider(Service_Provider_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_DataSource(DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Plant(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type)
REFERENCES IL_Order_Dtl(Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Product(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Warehouse(Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(UOM_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Unit_Of_Measurement(UOM_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

  Voucher_Line_Amount decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Fiscal_Year int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  Pay_Status_Code varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Product_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Gross_Amount decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Open_Amount decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,

  Tax_Amount decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,

  Base_Currency_Code varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,

  Total_Voucher_Amount decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Supplier_Invoice_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Purchase_Order_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Purchase_Order_Line_Number varchar(15) DEFAULT NULL,

  BNumber02 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  BDateTime01 datetime DEFAULT NULL,

  Updated_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (Company_Id,Voucher_Number,Voucher_Type,Voucher_Line_Number,Pay_Item_Extension_No,DataSource_Id),

  KEY IL_Account_Payable_FKIndex4 (UOM_Id,DataSource_Id),

  KEY IL_Account_Payable_idxkey (Acct_Payable_Key),
  KEY IL_Account_Payable_FKIndex6 (Plant_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Account_Payable_FKIndex7 (Company_Id,DataSource_Id)
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_Production (
  Prod_Plan_Id varchar(200) NOT NULL,

  DataSource_Id varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  Production_Key bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  Planned_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Plant_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Warehouse_Id varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  ShopFloor_Id varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  Machine_Id varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  Product_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Prod_Planned_Qty decimal(24,7) DEFAULT NULL,
  Prod_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Prod_Actual_Qty decimal(24,7) DEFAULT NULL,
  Unit_Price decimal(24,12) DEFAULT NULL,
  Planned_Staus_Code varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Prod_Status_Code varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Planned_Prod_Hours decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Prod_Hours decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  HourPerPrice decimal(24,12) DEFAULT NULL,
  Scrap_Qty decimal(24,7) DEFAULT NULL,
  Production_Revenue decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Resource_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Bcharacter01 varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Bcharacter02 varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  BNumber01 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  BNumber02 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  BDateTime01 datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  BBoolean bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Added_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Added_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  Updated_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Updated_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (Prod_Plan_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Production_ProdKey (Production_Key),
  KEY IL_Production_FKIndex1 (DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Production_FKIndex3 (ShopFloor_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Production_FKIndex5 (Plant_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Production_FKIndex6 (Resource_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Production_FKIndex9 (Product_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY Warehouse_Id (Warehouse_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY Machine_Id (Machine_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  CONSTRAINT IL_Production_ibfk_1 FOREIGN KEY (DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_DataSource (DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Production_ibfk_2 FOREIGN KEY (Warehouse_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Warehouse (Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Production_ibfk_3 FOREIGN KEY (ShopFloor_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_ShopFloor (ShopFloor_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Production_ibfk_4 FOREIGN KEY (Machine_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Machine (Machine_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Production_ibfk_5 FOREIGN KEY (Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Plant (Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Production_ibfk_6 FOREIGN KEY (Resource_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Resource (Resource_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Production_ibfk_7 FOREIGN KEY (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Product (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- Holds the Capacity details for the Warehouse for each Product on the bin.
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IL_Inventory (
Inventory_Number VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'System Generated Batch Number or Stock number that identifies the Inventory system' ,
Inventory_Date DATETIME  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Stock date or Inventory Stored date' ,
Company_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Plant company id details that having inventory storage available' ,
DataSource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded' ,
Inventory_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key + PK' ,
Plant_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Plant details of the  storage system available' ,
Warehouse_ID VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Warehouse /Department/Branch where the product stored' ,
Bin_Id VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Areas/place/Rack within each warehouse/Branch that product got stored.' ,
Product_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Product id that stored in stock/Storage location' ,
Customer_ID VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Customer id that stock produced.' ,
Order_Number VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Sales Order number that product stored' ,
Order_LineNumber VARCHAR(15)  NULL   COMMENT 'Sales Order line number that need to track agaist the SO' ,
Order_Type VARCHAR(50)  NULL  ,
OnHand_Qty NUMERIC(24,7)  NULL   COMMENT 'On hand Quantity' ,
Obsolescence_Flag BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Obsolescence details' ,
StockOut BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Is stock available or not' ,
Unit_Price NUMERIC(24,12)  NULL   COMMENT 'Cost per Unit to identify the inventory Value' ,
UOM_Id VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Unit of measurment(UOM) that need to identify the Case or Box details.' ,
Material_Diverted_Flag BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'If Product got diverted or' ,
Base_Currency_Code VARCHAR(10)  NULL  ,
Transaction_Currency_Code VARCHAR(10)  NULL  ,
Exchange_Rate NUMERIC(24,12)  NULL  ,
BCharacter01 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BCharacter02 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber01 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BDateTime01 DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BBoolean BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated User'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Inventory_Number, Inventory_Date, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Warehouse_Detail_FKIndex1(Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Warehouse_Detail_FKIndex3(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Warehouse_Detail_FKIndex4(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Warehouse_Detail_FKIndex8(Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Warehouse_Detail_FKIndex5(Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_FKIndex6(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_FKIndex7(DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_FKIndex8(Base_Currency_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_FKIndex9(Transaction_Currency_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_indxkey(Inventory_Key),
FOREIGN KEY(Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Warehouse(Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Plant(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)

ON UPDATE NO ACTION,

ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,

CREATE TABLE IL_Transport_Logistic (

ON UPDATE NO ACTION,

ON DELETE NO ACTION

ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,

CREATE TABLE IL_Order_Release (
  Order_Rel_Num varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Source system Order release number',
  Company_Id varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Company name that SO released',
  DataSource_Id varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded',
  Order_Number varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Order number for release',
  Order_LineNumber varchar(15) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Order line number for release',
  Order_Type varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  Order_Release_Key bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate key  + Auto increment',
  Product_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Product that ordered for release',
  Plant_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Warehouse_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Release_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Date of release the product',
  Release_Qty bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Number of quantity released',
  Release_Status varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Release status',
  MTS_Flag bit(1) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'To identfiy the SO is for Make To Stock or Make to Order',
  Insured_Flg bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Requested_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Rel_Handling_Amount decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Insured_Amt decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  BCharacter01 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BCharacter02 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber01 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber02 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BDateTime01 datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BBoolean bit(1) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  Added_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record insert/created date or sysdate',
  Added_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Added user',
  Updated_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate',
  Updated_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Updated user',
  PRIMARY KEY (Order_Rel_Num,Company_Id,DataSource_Id,Order_Number,Order_LineNumber),
  KEY IL_Order_Release_FKIndex2 (Order_Number,Order_LineNumber,Company_Id,DataSource_Id,Order_Type),
  KEY IL_Order_Release_FKIndex3 (Product_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Order_Release_FKIndex4 (Release_Status),
  KEY IL_Order_Release_Relesekey (Order_Release_Key),
  KEY IL_Order_Release_FKIndex6 (Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Order_Release_FKIndex5 (DataSource_Id),
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Release_ibfk_1 FOREIGN KEY (Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type) REFERENCES IL_Order_Dtl (Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Release_ibfk_2 FOREIGN KEY (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Product (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Release_ibfk_3 FOREIGN KEY (Release_Status) REFERENCES IL_Status (Status_Code) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Release_ibfk_4 FOREIGN KEY (Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Company (Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Order_Release_ibfk_5 FOREIGN KEY (DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_DataSource (DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_Job (
  Job_Number varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Uniquely identified  Work Order Code or Job Number',
  Company_Id varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Company Code',
  DataSource_Id varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded',
  Order_Type varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  Job_Description varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Description of  the job',
  Job_Key bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key',
  Plant_ID varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Plant or Bussiness Unit job allocated',
  Product_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Product Details of the Job /Work Order Allowcated',
  Sales_Order_Number varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Sales Order Number',
  Sales_Order_LineNumber varchar(15) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Sales Order Line Number that SO created for Product',
  Quote_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Quote_Line_Number varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Shipped_date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Unit_Of_Measure varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Unit of Measure of the Quantity',
  Requested_Qty decimal(24,7) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Total Requested quantity of the product for sales order',
  Completed_Qty decimal(24,7) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Total completed quantity of the product for sales order',
  Start_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Start date of the Job',
  Job_Requested_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Requested Job due date',
  Job_Due_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Job due date',
  Job_Completion_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Job completion date',
  Job_Type varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Type of the Job',
  Job_Status_Code varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Status of the Job or WO',
  Order_Release_Id varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Order Release number details',
  Warehouse_Id varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Ware house Id where the Product is stored',
  BCharacter01 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BCharacter02 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber01 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber02 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BDateTime01 datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BBoolean bit(1) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  Added_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record insert/created date or sysdate',
  Added_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Added user',
  Updated_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate',
  Updated_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Updated user',
  PRIMARY KEY (Job_Number,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Job_Idx_JobKey (Job_Key),
  KEY IL_Job_Idx_ReqQty (Requested_Qty),
  KEY IL_Job_Idx_CompQty (Completed_Qty),
  KEY IL_Job_Idx_Start_date (Start_Date),
  KEY IL_Job_Idx_Req_due_dt (Job_Requested_Date),
  KEY IL_Job_Idx_JobDuedt (Job_Due_Date),
  KEY IL_Job_Idx_JobCompletion_dt (Job_Completion_Date),
  KEY IL_Job_Idx_Jobtype (Job_Type),
  KEY IL_Job_FKIndex1 (Plant_ID,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Job_FKIndex3 (Product_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Job_FKIndex4 (Job_Status_Code),
  KEY IL_Job_FKIndex5 (Sales_Order_Number,Sales_Order_LineNumber,Company_Id,DataSource_Id,Order_Type),
  KEY IL_Job_FKIndex7 (Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Job_FKIndex6 (DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Job_FKIndex8 (Quote_Number,Quote_Line_Number,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  CONSTRAINT IL_Job_ibfk_1 FOREIGN KEY (Plant_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Plant (Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Job_ibfk_2 FOREIGN KEY (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Product (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Job_ibfk_3 FOREIGN KEY (Job_Status_Code) REFERENCES IL_Status (Status_Code) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Job_ibfk_4 FOREIGN KEY (Sales_Order_Number, Sales_Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type) REFERENCES IL_Order_Dtl (Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Job_ibfk_5 FOREIGN KEY (Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Company (Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Job_ibfk_6 FOREIGN KEY (DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_DataSource (DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_JobMtl (
Job_Number VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Job or Work Order number' ,

Plant_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Plant details.' ,

Job_Mtl_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate  Key + PK' ,
Requested_Qty NUMERIC(24,7)  NULL   COMMENT 'Total requested quantity' ,
Estimated_Scrap NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Discarded or removed from service product qty' ,
Currency_Code VARCHAR(10)  NULL   COMMENT 'Currency Code that Estimation cost defined.' ,
Est_Unit_Cost NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Estimated unit cost' ,
Est_Mtl_Unit_Cost NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Estimated metirial cost' ,
Est_Bur_Unit_Cost NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Estimatied Burnt cost' ,
Est_Labour_Unit_Cost NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Estimated Labour Cost' ,
Est_Sub_Unit_Cost NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Estimated Sub unit cost' ,
BCharacter01 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BCharacter02 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber01 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BDateTime01 DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BBoolean BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Job_Number, Company_Id, Plant_Id, Product_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_JobMtl_FKIndex2(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_JobMtl_FKIndex3(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_JobMtl_FKIndex4(Job_Number, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_JobMtl_FKIndex7(Currency_Code)  ,
INDEX IL_JobMtl_FKIndex5(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_JobMtl_FKIndex6(DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_JobMtl_index11986(Job_Mtl_Key),
FOREIGN KEY(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Plant(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Product(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Job_Number, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Job(Job_Number, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Currency_Code)
REFERENCES IL_Currency(Currency_Code)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Company(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_DataSource(DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- Holds the Retrun quantiity transaction details for the Order and customer.
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IL_Returns (
Order_Number VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Order Number that linked to Sales to track the details' ,
Order_LineNumber VARCHAR(15)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Order line number that linked from Retruned' ,
Order_Type VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL  ,
Return_Date DATETIME  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Date of the product Returned by customer' ,
DataSource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded' ,
Return_Key INTEGER UNSIGNED  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate key + PK' ,
Company_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL   COMMENT 'Company details' ,
Product_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Product code/Item Code/Short Descr that Retruned' ,
Plant_ID VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Plant details' ,
Customer_ID VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Customer that Order retruned' ,
Return_Qty NUMERIC(24,7)  NULL   COMMENT 'Quantity Retruned by the customer' ,
Unit_Price NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Unit Price of the Product' ,
Retrun_Amount NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Total Retruned amount of the Line' ,
Retrun_Reason_Type VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Type of the Retrun reason' ,
Return_Reason VARCHAR(200)  NULL   COMMENT 'Reason for retruning' ,
Base_Currency_Code VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Base currency code for Caluclation' ,
Transaction_Currency_Code VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Transaction currency details' ,
Exchange_Rate NUMERIC(24,12)  NULL   COMMENT 'Exchange rate of the currency between base currency and transaction currency' ,
BCharacter01 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BCharacter02 VARCHAR(100)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber01 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BDateTime01 DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
BBoolean BIT  NULL   COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose' ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record insert/CREATEd date or sysdate' ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Added user' ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL   COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate' ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL   COMMENT 'Updated user'   ,
PRIMARY KEY(Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Order_Type, Return_Date, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Returns_FKIndex2(Plant_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Returns_FKIndex3(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Returns_FKIndex4(Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type)  ,
INDEX IL_Returns_FKIndex5(Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Returns_FKIndex6(Retrun_Reason_Type)  ,
INDEX IL_Returns_FKIndex8(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Returns_FKIndex7(DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Returns_idxkey(Return_Key),
FOREIGN KEY(Plant_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Plant(Plant_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Product(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type)
REFERENCES IL_Order_Dtl(Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Customer(Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Retrun_Reason_Type)
REFERENCES IL_Retrun_Reason_Type(Retrun_Reason_Type)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Company(Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_DataSource(DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION)
