  Added_User varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Updated_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Updated_User varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (Company_Id,PO_Receive_Line_Number,DataSource_Id,PO_Number,PO_Line_Number,PO_Type),
  KEY IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_FKIndex2 (UOM_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_FKIndex3 (DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_FKIndex4 (Bin_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id,Warehouse_ID),
  KEY IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_FKIndex5 (Supplier_ID,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_FKIndex6 (Product_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_FKIndex7 (Warehouse_ID,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_FKIndex8 (Plant_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_FKIndex9 (Receive_Type),
  KEY IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_FKIndex10 (Payment_Terms_Code,DataSource_Id,Company_Id),
  KEY IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_idxkey (PO_Receive_Dtl_Key),
  CONSTRAINT IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_ibfk_1 FOREIGN KEY (UOM_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Unit_Of_Measurement (UOM_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_ibfk_2 FOREIGN KEY (DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_DataSource (DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_ibfk_3 FOREIGN KEY (Bin_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Warehouse_ID) REFERENCES IL_Bin (Bin_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Warehouse_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_ibfk_4 FOREIGN KEY (Supplier_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Supplier (Supplier_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_ibfk_5 FOREIGN KEY (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Product (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_ibfk_6 FOREIGN KEY (Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Warehouse (Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_ibfk_7 FOREIGN KEY (Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Plant (Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_ibfk_8 FOREIGN KEY (Receive_Type) REFERENCES IL_Receive_Type (Receive_Type) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_PO_Receive_Dtl_ibfk_9 FOREIGN KEY (Payment_Terms_Code, DataSource_Id, Company_Id) REFERENCES IL_Payment_Terms_Code (Payment_Terms_Code, DataSource_Id, Company_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- Holds Shipped Quantity transaction data of the customer.
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IL_Shipments (
  Shipment_Number varchar(100) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Shippment Number Uniquely identifed by the System',
  Company_Id varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT 'SO Shipped Company',
  Plant_ID varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT 'SO Plant or Bussiness unit',
  Order_Number varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Sales order id mapped to Sales oder dtl table',
  Order_LineNumber varchar(15) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Sales order id mapped to Sales oder dtl table',
  Order_Type varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  Shipped_Date datetime NOT NULL COMMENT 'Date Shipped the product to customer/Distributor',
  DataSource_Id varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded',
  Shipment_Key int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key',
  Product_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Product or Item Code / Short descr of the SO',
  Job_Number varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Job Number Related to Production',
  Order_Rel_Num varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'SO Release Number.',
  Customer_ID varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Primary Customer details of the SO',
  Warehouse_ID varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Warehouse details',
  Promise_To_Ship_date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Date of Shippment promise.',
  Order_Pickedup_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Data of Picked up for shippment',
  Shipped_Qty decimal(24,7) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Number of quantity shipped to customer/Distributor',
  Unit_Price decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Unit Price of the Product',
  Shipped_Amount decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Shipped Order Line Amount',
  Handling_Cost decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Invoice_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Date of bill/Invoice generated',
  Cancelled_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Cancelled Date of Shippment',
  Cancelled_Qty decimal(24,7) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Total number Qty cacelled for shippment of the product',
  Base_Currency_Code varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Base Currency code of the Company',
  Transaction_Currency_Code varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Transaction Currency code of the Company',
  Exchange_Rate decimal(24,12) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Exchange /Conversion Rate of the Currency',
  Mode_Of_Transport varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Transport mode through Air,Road,Water,Pipeline',
  Container_Id varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Container Details',
  Reason_Code varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Reason code for Cancel or on hold',
  BCharacter01 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BCharacter02 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber01 decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber02 decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BDateTime01 datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BBoolean bit(1) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  Added_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record insert/created date or sysdate',
  Added_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Added user',
  Updated_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate',
  Updated_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Updated user',
  PRIMARY KEY (Shipment_Number,Company_Id,Plant_ID,Order_Number,Order_LineNumber,Order_Type,Shipped_Date,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Shipments_FKIndex2 (Plant_ID,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Shipments_FKIndex3 (Order_Number,Order_LineNumber,Company_Id,DataSource_Id,Order_Type),
  KEY IL_Shipments_FKIndex4 (Order_Rel_Num,Company_Id,DataSource_Id,Order_Number,Order_LineNumber),
  KEY IL_Shipments_FKIndex5 (Product_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Shipments_FKIndex6 (Customer_ID,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Shipments_FKIndex7 (Job_Number,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Shipments_FKIndex8 (Warehouse_ID,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Shipments_FKIndex10 (Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Shipments_FKIndex9 (DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Shipments_indxkey (Shipment_Key),
  CONSTRAINT IL_Shipments_ibfk_1 FOREIGN KEY (Plant_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Plant (Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Shipments_ibfk_2 FOREIGN KEY (Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type) REFERENCES IL_Order_Dtl (Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Shipments_ibfk_3 FOREIGN KEY (Order_Rel_Num, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Number, Order_LineNumber) REFERENCES IL_Order_Release (Order_Rel_Num, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Number, Order_LineNumber) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Shipments_ibfk_4 FOREIGN KEY (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Product (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Shipments_ibfk_5 FOREIGN KEY (Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Customer (Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Shipments_ibfk_6 FOREIGN KEY (Job_Number, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Job (Job_Number, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Shipments_ibfk_7 FOREIGN KEY (Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Warehouse (Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Shipments_ibfk_8 FOREIGN KEY (Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Company (Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Shipments_ibfk_9 FOREIGN KEY (DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_DataSource (DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- Holds the Invoice Billing Data for Ordered product.
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IL_Invoice (
  Company_Id varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Company Id details',
  Invoice_Number varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Invoice number uniquely genereted for Order',
  Invoice_Line_Number varchar(15) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Invoice Line number for Each product that invoiced',
  Order_Number varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Order number of that invoice processed',
  Order_LineNumber varchar(15) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Order Line number that invoice processed',
  Order_Type varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  DataSource_Id varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded',
  Invoice_Key bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key   + Auto Generated',
  Invoice_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Date  of invoice generated',
  Plant_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Plant or Bussiness unit of the invoice generated',
  Product_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Name of the product that Order executed',
  Customer_ID varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Customer code or Id that Invoice Generated',
  Order_Rel_Num varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Order Release number details',
  Order_Quantity decimal(24,7) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Total Qty orderd by the customer',
  Shipped_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Date that order got shipped',
  Shipped_Quantity decimal(24,7) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Total quntity shipped to customer',
  Unit_Price decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Unit price of the Order on product',
  Invoice_Status varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Status of the invoice',
  Warehouse_ID varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ware house or branch that order picked up',
  UOM_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Batch_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Posted_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Sent_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Recorded_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Due_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Ship_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Paid_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  GL_Posted_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Invoice_Cancelled_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Non_Invoice_Flag bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Posted_Flag bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Posting_Hold_Flag bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Fiscal_Period int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  Fiscal_Year int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  Misc_Amount decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Invoice_Balance decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Unposted_Balance decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Invoice_Line_Amount decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Invoice_Amount decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Invoice Amount',
  Tax_Amount decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Total tax applied',
  Discount_Amount decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Discount Amount',
  Total_Amount decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Total = Invoice_Amt-Discount_amount+Tax',
  Invoice_Type varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Type of the invoice',
  Distribution_channel varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Distribution channel details',
  Sales_RespCode varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Sales Representive Code that order booked',
  Invoice_Comment varchar(5000) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Any comments for that invoice',
  Base_Currency_Code varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Base Currency code that Invoice genrated',
  Transaction_Currency_Code varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Transaction currency code that need to convert with base currency',
  Exchange_Rate decimal(24,12) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Conversion exchange rate for Base currency and Transactional currency',
  BCharacter01 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BCharacter02 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber01 decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber02 decimal(18,2) unsigned zerofill DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BDateTime01 datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BBoolean bit(1) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  Added_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record insert/created date or sysdate',
  Added_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Added user',
  Updated_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate',
  Updated_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Updated user',
  PRIMARY KEY (Company_Id,Invoice_Number,Invoice_Line_Number,Order_Number,Order_LineNumber,Order_Type,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Invoice_FKIndex2 (Customer_ID,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Invoice_FKIndex3 (Product_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Invoice_FKIndex4 (Order_Number,Order_LineNumber,Company_Id,DataSource_Id,Order_Type),
  KEY IL_Invoice_FKIndex11 (Invoice_Status),
  KEY IL_Invoice_InvoiceKey (Invoice_Key),
  KEY IL_Invoice_FKIndex5 (Base_Currency_Code),
  KEY IL_Invoice_FKIndex6 (Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Invoice_FKIndex7 (Order_Rel_Num,Company_Id,DataSource_Id,Order_Number,Order_LineNumber),
  KEY IL_Invoice_FKIndex8 (Plant_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Invoice_FKIndex9 (Warehouse_ID,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY IL_Invoice_FKIndex10 (DataSource_Id),
  CONSTRAINT IL_Invoice_ibfk_1 FOREIGN KEY (Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Customer (Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Invoice_ibfk_10 FOREIGN KEY (DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_DataSource (DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Invoice_ibfk_2 FOREIGN KEY (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Product (Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Invoice_ibfk_3 FOREIGN KEY (Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type) REFERENCES IL_Order_Dtl (Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Invoice_ibfk_4 FOREIGN KEY (Invoice_Status) REFERENCES IL_Status (Status_Code) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Invoice_ibfk_5 FOREIGN KEY (Base_Currency_Code) REFERENCES IL_Currency (Currency_Code) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Invoice_ibfk_6 FOREIGN KEY (Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Company (Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Invoice_ibfk_8 FOREIGN KEY (Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Plant (Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT IL_Invoice_ibfk_9 FOREIGN KEY (Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) REFERENCES IL_Warehouse (Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_Inventory_Transfer (
Transaction_Number VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL  ,
Transaction_Line_Number VARCHAR(15)  NOT NULL  ,
Transfer_Type VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL  ,
DataSource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL  ,
Inv_Trf_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT,
Transaction_Date DATETIME  NULL  ,
Product_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Batch_No VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
From_Company_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
From_Plant_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
From_Warehouse_Id VARCHAR(50)  NULL  ,
From_Bin_Id VARCHAR(50)  NULL  ,
From_Location_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
From_Qty NUMERIC(24,7)  NULL  ,
From_Unit_Price NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
From_UOM_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
From_Inv_Transaction_Value NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
To_Company_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
To_Plant_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
To_Warehouse_Id VARCHAR(50)  NULL  ,
To_Bin_Id VARCHAR(50)  NULL  ,
To_Location_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
To_Qty NUMERIC(24,7)  NULL  ,
To_UOM_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
To_Unit_Price NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
To_Inv_Transaction_Value NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
Resource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Reason_Code VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Transfer_Reason VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Base_Currency_Code VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Transaction_Currency_Code VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Exchange_Rate NUMERIC(24,12)  NULL  ,
BCharacter01 VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
BCharacter02 VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
BNumber01 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
BDateTime01 DATETIME  NULL  ,
BBoolean BIT  NULL  ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL  ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL  ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL  ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL    ,
PRIMARY KEY(Transaction_Number, Transaction_Line_Number, Transfer_Type, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_Transfer_FKIndex1(From_Bin_Id, From_Company_Id, DataSource_Id, From_Warehouse_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_Transfer_FKIndex2(To_Bin_Id, To_Company_Id, DataSource_Id, To_Warehouse_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_Transfer_FKIndex3(From_Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_Transfer_FKIndex4(To_Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_Transfer_FKIndex5(From_Plant_Id, From_Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_Transfer_FKIndex6(To_Plant_Id, To_Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_Transfer_FKIndex7(From_UOM_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_Transfer_FKIndex8(To_UOM_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_Transfer_FKIndex9(Resource_Id, From_Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_Transfer_FKIndex10(DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_Transfer_FKIndex11(Product_Id, From_Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Inventory_Transfer_Key(Inv_Trf_Key),
FOREIGN KEY(From_Bin_Id, From_Company_Id, DataSource_Id, From_Warehouse_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Bin(Bin_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Warehouse_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(To_Bin_Id, To_Company_Id, DataSource_Id, To_Warehouse_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Bin(Bin_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Warehouse_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(From_Warehouse_ID, From_Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Warehouse(Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(To_Warehouse_ID, To_Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Warehouse(Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(From_Plant_Id, From_Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Plant(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(To_Plant_Id, To_Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Plant(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(From_UOM_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Unit_Of_Measurement(UOM_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(To_UOM_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Unit_Of_Measurement(UOM_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Resource_Id, From_Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Resource(Resource_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_DataSource(DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Product_Id, From_Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Product(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;
CREATE TABLE IL_Pick_Details (
Company_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL  ,
Pick_Slip_Number VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL  ,
Picked_Date DATETIME  NOT NULL  ,
DataSource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NOT NULL  ,
Pick_Dtl_Key BIGINT  NOT NULL   AUTO_INCREMENT,
Scheduled_Pick_Date DATETIME  NULL  ,
Sales_Order_Number VARCHAR(50)  NULL  ,
Sales_Order_LineNumber VARCHAR(15)  NULL  ,
Order_Type VARCHAR(50)  NULL  ,
Customer_ID VARCHAR(50)  NULL  ,
Batch_Number VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Pick_Type VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Plant_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Warehouse_ID VARCHAR(50)  NULL  ,
Bin_Id VARCHAR(50)  NULL  ,
Product_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Pickup_From VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Dock_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
UOM_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Orderd_Qty NUMERIC(24,7)  NULL  ,
Planned_Pick_Qty NUMERIC(24,7)  NULL  ,
Picked_Qty NUMERIC(24,7)  NULL  ,
PickUp_Status_Code VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Pick_Resource_Id VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
Resource_Pick_Hours NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
Pick_Resource_Cost NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
Planned_Delivery_Date DATETIME  NULL  ,
Deliver_Date DATETIME  NULL  ,
BCharacter01 VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
BCharacter02 VARCHAR(200)  NULL  ,
BNumber01 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
BNumber02 NUMERIC(18,2)  NULL  ,
BDateTime01 DATETIME  NULL  ,
BBoolean01 BIT  NULL  ,
Added_Date DATETIME  NULL  ,
Added_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL  ,
Updated_Date DATETIME  NULL  ,
Updated_User VARCHAR(50)  NULL    ,
PRIMARY KEY(Company_Id, Pick_Slip_Number, Picked_Date, DataSource_Id)  ,

INDEX IL_Pick_Details_FKIndex2(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Pick_Details_FKIndex3(Bin_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Warehouse_ID)  ,
INDEX IL_Pick_Details_FKIndex4(Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Pick_Details_FKIndex5(Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Pick_Details_FKIndex6(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Pick_Details_FKIndex7(Pick_Resource_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Pick_Details_FKIndex8(UOM_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Pick_Details_FKIndex9(Dock_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Pick_Details_FKIndex10(DataSource_Id)  ,
INDEX IL_Pick_Details_FKIndex11(Pick_Type)  ,
INDEX IL_Pick_Details_inxkey(Pick_Dtl_Key),
FOREIGN KEY(Sales_Order_Number, Sales_Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type)
REFERENCES IL_Order_Dtl(Order_Number, Order_LineNumber, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Order_Type)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Plant(Plant_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Bin_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Warehouse_ID)
REFERENCES IL_Bin(Bin_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id, Warehouse_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Warehouse(Warehouse_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Customer(Customer_ID, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Product(Product_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Pick_Resource_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Resource(Resource_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(UOM_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Unit_Of_Measurement(UOM_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Dock_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_Dock(Dock_Id, Company_Id, DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(DataSource_Id)
REFERENCES IL_DataSource(DataSource_Id)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
FOREIGN KEY(Pick_Type)
REFERENCES IL_Pick_Type(Pick_Type)
ON DELETE NO ACTION
ON UPDATE NO ACTION
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS  fn_base_cur_amt;

CREATE FUNCTION fn_base_cur_amt(v_txn_Date datetime ,v_Base_Currency_Code varchar(10),v_Amount decimal(18,2)) RETURNS decimal(18,2)
    READS SQL DATA
fun_label:BEGIN

DECLARE v_Base_Curr_Amount decimal(18,2);
SET v_Base_Curr_Amount = 0.0;

IF v_Amount = 0 OR v_Amount IS NULL THEN
		  RETURN 0.0;
          LEAVE fun_label;
END IF;
     
SELECT coalesce(v_Amount* IL_Currency_Rate.EXCHANGE_RATE,0.0) into v_Base_Curr_Amount
FROM IL_Currency_Rate IL_Currency_Rate
JOIN IL_Client_Currency ON  IL_Currency_Rate.To_Currency_Code=IL_Client_Currency.Currency_Code 
WHERE IL_Currency_Rate.From_Currency_Code = v_Base_Currency_Code 
AND IL_Currency_Rate.CURRENCY_START_PERIOD <= v_txn_Date   
AND IL_Currency_Rate.CURRENCY_END_PERIOD>= v_txn_Date
AND  IL_Client_Currency.Rpt_Base_Currency_Flag=1;
RETURN coalesce(v_Base_Curr_Amount,0.0);
END;


/* pipedrive ILs 16 total IL_Activity, IL_Activity_Type, IL_Company_CRM, IL_Currency_CRM, IL_Deals, IL_Goals, IL_Note, IL_Organization, IL_PipeLine, IL_Person_Phone, IL_Person_Email, IL_Persons, IL_Product_CRM, IL_Product_Deal,IL_Product_Price, IL_Stages, IL_User*/


CREATE TABLE IL_Activity (
  Activity_Id varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  Company_Id varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  DataSource_Id varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  Activity_Key bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  User_Id varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Deal_Id varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Organization_Id varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Person_Id varchar(250) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Activity_Done_Flag bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Activity_Type varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Activity_Due_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Activity_Duration datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Marked_As_Done_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Act_Subject varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Active_Flag bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Person_Name varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Organization_Name varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Note varchar(5000) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Deal_Title varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Reference_Type varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Reference_Id varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Due_Time datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Activity_Add_Time datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Assigned_To_User_Id varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Created_By_User_Id varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  BCharacter01 varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  BCharacter02 varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  BNumber01 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  BNumber02 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  BDateTime01 datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  BBoolean bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Added_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Added_User varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Updated_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Updated_User varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (Activity_Id,Company_Id,DataSource_Id),
  KEY Activity_Key (Activity_Key)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_Activity_Type (
  Activity_Type_Id varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,

  Active_Flag bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Color varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Custom_Flag bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Seq_Num bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  Key_String varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Icon_Key varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  BCharacter01 varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  BCharacter02 varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  BNumber01 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  BNumber02 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  BDateTime01 datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  BBoolean bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  Added_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Added_User varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  Updated_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  Updated_User varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,

  KEY IL_Activity_Type (Activity_Type_Key)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE IL_Company_CRM (
  Company_Id varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'Code of the company/Id of the company with Uniquely identified.',
  DataSource_Id varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded',
  Company_Key bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrorgate key',
  XRef_Company_Key bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  Company_Name varchar(200) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Name of the Company',
  Address1 varchar(100) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Address of the Company',
  Address2 varchar(100) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Address of the Company',
  City varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'City of the Company',
  Zipcode varchar(30) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'ZipCode of the Company',
  Email varchar(100) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Email Address of the Company',
  State varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'State of the Company',
  Country varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Country details',
  Region varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Region of the company',
  Sub_Region varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Sub Region details',
  Currency_Code varchar(10) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Base Currency Code details',
  Hierarchy_Lvl1 varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Hierarchy levles',
  Hierarchy_Lvl2 varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Hierarchy levles',
  Hierarchy_Lvl3 varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Hierarchy levles',
  Hierarchy_Lvl4 varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Hierarchy levles',

CREATE TABLE XRef_IL_Bin (
  XRef_Bin_Key bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'Surrogate Key + PK',
  Bin_Id varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Bin Location Id details at the Department',
  Company_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  DataSource_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded',
  Warehouse_Id varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Branch Details that Bin located',
  Bin_Name varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Name of the Bin Location.',
  Bin_Description varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Description of the Bin',
  Plant_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Plant that Bin located',
  Aisle_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Location_Type varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Zone_Location_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Bin_Capacity decimal(24,6) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Capacity of the Bin',
  Location varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Location of the Bin',
  Bin_Usable_Length decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Bin_Usable_Width decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Bin_Usable_Height decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Usable_Size_UOM varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Bin_Capable_Weight decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Capable_Weight_UOM varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  BCharacter01 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BCharacter02 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber01 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber02 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BDateTime01 datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BBoolean bit(1) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  Added_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record insert/created date or sysdate',
  Added_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Added user',
  Updated_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate',
  Updated_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Updated user',
  PRIMARY KEY (XRef_Bin_Key)
)ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci;

  DataSource_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'To Identify the Multiple Source System/Data mangement System that got loaded',
  Warehouse_Name varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Warehouse Name',
  Plant_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Bussiness Unit or Plant that Branch or Warehouse available',
  Warehouse_Type varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Type of warehouse grouped together',
  Warehouse_Height decimal(24,8) DEFAULT NULL,
  Warehouse_Width decimal(24,8) DEFAULT NULL,
  Warehouse_Length decimal(24,8) DEFAULT NULL,
  UOM_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Warehouse_Usable_Width decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Warehouse_Usable_Height decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Warehouse_Usable_Length decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Usable_UOM_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Warehouse_Usable_Weight decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  Usable_Weight_UOM_Id varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  Location varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Location details',
  BCharacter01 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BCharacter02 varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber01 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BNumber02 decimal(18,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BDateTime01 datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  BBoolean bit(1) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Extract column for any missing column mapping purpose',
  Added_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record insert/created date or sysdate',
  Added_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Added user',
  Updated_Date datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Source Record Updated date or sysdate',
  Updated_User varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Updated user',
  PRIMARY KEY (XRef_Warehouse_Key)
  )ENGINE = InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8 COLLATE = utf8_unicode_ci COMMENT='Holds Warehouse  Master table data information with location details.';
